              <span class="article-card__headline-clamp">
               SALTZMAN: Tech provides free ways to enjoy a spring ‘staycation’
              </span>
             </h3>
             <p class="article-card__excerpt">
              Between travel restrictions, COVID’s third wave, and the financial strain caused by the pandemic,  many will be trading their annual spring getaway for a “staycation.”

          <div class="article-card__content">
           <div class="article-card__details">
            <div class="article-card__meta-top">
             <span class="article-card__category">
              <a class="article-card__category-link" href="/category/basketball/">

               </span>

            <a aria-label="RAPTORS BLOG: On the foul disparity, the return of OG, the 6-man race" class="article-card__link" href="/sports/basketball/raptors-blog-on-the-foul-disparity-the-return-of-og-the-6-man-race">
             <h3 class="article-card__headline text-size--extra-large--sm-up" title="RAPTORS BLOG: On the foul disparity, the return of OG, the 6-man race">
              <span class="article-card__headline-clamp">
               RAPTORS BLOG: On the foul disparity, the return of OG, the 6-man race
              </span>
             </h3>
             <p class="article-card__excerpt">
              Back at full strength the Toronto Raptors looked much more like the team they are when everyone is available — one that can at least hang with any opponent, even the NBA-leading Utah Jazz. Unfortunately their season-long issues in the clutch reared their ugly head again with a series of bad decisions late, followed by a fourth heart-breaking Pascal Siakam miss on a potential game-tier or game-winner this season. Luck just hasn’t gone Toronto’s way in this trying season and they’re now closer to 13th in the conference than to eighth, though things can change quickly.
             </p>
            </a>
            <div class="article-card__meta-bottom">
             <span class="article-card__time">
              1 day ago
             </span>
             <span class="article-card__category">
              <a class="article-card__category-link" href="/category/basketball/">
               <span>
                Basketball
               </span>
              </a>
             </span>
            </div>
           </div>

             <h3 class="article-card__headline text-size--extra-large--sm-up" title="EDITORIAL: Tories reject O'Toole on climate change">
              <span class="article-card__headline-clamp">
               EDITORIAL: Tories reject O'Toole on climate change
              </span>
             </h3>
             <p class="article-card__excerpt">
              By failing to pass a motherhood motion at their policy convention stating that “climate change is real” on Saturday, the federal Conservatives shot themselves and party leader Erin O’Toole in the foot.
             </p>
